    function RefreshOnDeleteItemRequisitions(PRId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var key = '';
        $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/DeleteItemDetailsPopup',
                         { MassOperationId: massOperationId, PRId: PRId },
                    key, function (result) {
                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount() {
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount",
            data: { prId: '4884' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result !== null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var tot = parseFloat(result.TotalAmount);
                    tot = tot.toFixed(2);
                    $("#RequisitionTotalAmount").text("$" + tot);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function DeleteItemRequisitions() {
        var prID = '4884';

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonDeactivate(function () { GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount(); }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteItemRequisitions(prID); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    $("#btnShopOnline__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var prID = '4884';
        var vendorID = '4';
        var data = { vendorID: vendorID };
        showSpinner();
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/IsEcommerceVendor',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "")
                        if (result) {

                            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/RedirectToVendor" + "?PRId=" + prID + "&amp;vendorID=" + vendorID + "&amp;ecommerceAction=" + 'edit' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3'+ "&amp;fromPopup=true");
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowAjaxMessage("Vendor is not an eCommerce Vendor", "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        }
                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnAdd__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var ecommerce = 'False';
        var prID = '4884';
        var vendorID = '4';
        var data = { vendorID: vendorID };
        var openPRItemPopupAddMode = false;

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/IsEcommerceVendor',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "")
                        if (result) {
                            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/RedirectToVendor" + "?PRId=" + prID + "&amp;vendorID=" + vendorID + "&amp;ecommerceAction=" + 'create' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
                        }
                        else {
                            openPRItemPopupAddMode = true;
                        }
                }
            }
        });
        if (openPRItemPopupAddMode == true) OpenPRItemPopupAddMode()
    });

    function OpenPRItemPopupAddMode()
    {
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: '4884', statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CreatePRItemPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowItemDetailsPopup")
            .SetIsModal(true)
            .SetContent(options)
            .SetHeight(500)
            .SetWidth(820)
            .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionItem)
            .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            .SetTitle("Add Purchase Requisition Line Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", null);
    }

    $('#btnEditAll__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click();
        }
        $('#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click();
    });

    $("#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });

    function ItemDetails(Id) {
        EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow(Id, null)
    }

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data, options;

        data = { PRId: '4884', prItemSequence: id, statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'PURCHASE_REQUISITION', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ItemDetailsPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowItemDetailsPopup")
   .SetIsModal(true)
   .SetContent(options)
   .SetHeight(500)
   .SetWidth(820)
   .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionItem)
   .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
   .SetTitle("Edit Purchase Requisition Line Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", null);
    }

    function ReturnFromRequisitionItem() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $('#btnCopy__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'N' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'R' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'S') {
            CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
        }
        else
        {
            if (prStatus == 'S' &amp;&amp; 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisitions') {
                CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
            }
            else{
                SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "CopyRequisition")
            }
        }
    });

    function CopyRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CopyRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '4884' },
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {

                        var newPRID = result.NewPRID;
                        if (newPRID != null)
                        {
                            var aptaDataViewSelection;
                            var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid != null)
                            {
                                aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            }
                            else{
                                aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                            }

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : newPRID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

                        if(grid != null)
                            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnUndoSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Undo Submit", "Are you sure you would like to undo submit and change the requisition status back to New?", function () { UndoSubmiRequisitionPopup(e) });
    });

    function UndoSubmiRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/UndoSubmitRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '4884' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != null &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '4884';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }

                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnWithdrawMyPR__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Withdraw", "Are you sure you would like to withdraw this requisition?", function () { WithdrawRequisitionPopup(e) });
    });

    function WithdrawRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/WithdrawRequisition",
            data: { prId: '4884' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    if(AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != null &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '4884', origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnApprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e);
    });

    function ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e) {

        var data = { prId: '4884' };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove",
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result.Success == false) {
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '', origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '', ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove: true },type:"POST"});
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Approve");
                    }

                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ApproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';
        var arr = selectedRowIds.split('~');

        var data = { approverId: approverId, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '0' };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/SingleRequisitionApproveAction",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == 1) {
                    var navigationID = 0;

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
                        ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition approved successfully.', "success");
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function closRequisitionActiveWindow(e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';

        var data, options;

        data = { approverId: approverId, requireMyAttention: false, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '0' , Ismultiple: false };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/DisapproveRequisition", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowDisapproveRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetonClose(function () {
           if ($('#IsDisapprovedProcessed').val() == 1)
           {
               SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Disapprove")
           }
       })
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Disapprove Requisition')
       .SetWidth(550)
       .SetHeight(150)
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "RequisitionApproval", null);

    }

    function RefreshPopupAfterDisapproveRequisition(e) {

        var navigationID = 0;

        if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
            closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success");
        }
        else{
            navigationID = '';
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        }

    }

    $('#btnDisapprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e);
    });

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })
